 wo bhoomihin hai or unhone teen bigha khet rehan par lekar fasal lagaai thi
 The rain left nothing
 heeralaal is gam main biimaar ho gaye hai
 They lie on the bed, but when the NDTV team reached to know their condition, they stood up for some help
 garmi main bhi shawl odh kar khet kii taraf chal die
 He expressed his sorrow by showing his ruined crop
 "halaat ek damme down ba, teen bighaa liye the kulhi naash kar diye
 Now we can not find Ka Mili Ka
 " Malik Yadav of the village has the same situation
 unhone do bigha khet kiraaye par liya tha or ab barbaad ho chuke anaaj main se kuch kaam laayak nikaalane kii koshish kar rahe hai
 He told us how the grains have rot due to water
 yahi haal saalik ram kaa bhi he
 At the same time we also got piercing the wasted crop
 piyaari ke ghar shaadi he or fasal barbaad ho gai
 She does not understand what to do? All roads are closed
 "teen bighaa ham khet le le rahali, hamare ghar jhatkal dana ba naahi, hamare ghar shaadi padal ba
 Now i am talking ghar main sab kehu roat-peett ba
 Oh God, the Kauna is in trouble
 " Chunna Lal, a farmer who cultivates pharna, came running to see us that he has come
 barbaad fasal kaa muyna kar rahe hai
 As soon as he came, he started insisting on walking towards his ruined farm, but immediately when we asked him about the farmers who took the paddy field, he immediately said, "I have met the farmer himself on the paddy field
" khet jiske naam he
 The Adhiyas have done plowing, the Bengalis have been planted, the Sura have been composted and they have spent their expenses
 milegaa to kastkaar ko milegaa, hamako kya milegaa
 We will die "tippaniyan Hundreds of villages such as Mahda, Chakka, Tilampur, Namapur, Varadih, Khonchwa, Akhri Chitouni of Banaras, including Jagdevpur, have poor farmers cultivating Bataiya and Rehan
 inkaa sabase bada dard yahi he ki kisi tarah paise juta kar, udhaar lekar inhone kheti kii or ab jab fasal nasht ho gai he to inhen muaavja bhi nahin milegi
 Not only this, the person who has the land will have to pay the mortgage amount
 ab ye unke raham-o-karam par hai
 This is a painful truth because the lifeless landless farmers who cultivate ren and bataiya are halfway alive without land and this time the rain has washed away all their hard work
 lihaaja unki jindagi ekadam bejaar ho chuki he
 The big question is: will such farmers get a place in the list of compensation? Are these farmers on the government's agenda or not? If not, then you can think yourself how will they live and if they are alive in any way, then how will they live? in kisaano kii sankhya kitni he iske aankade main ulajhane ke bajaay yahi kahana zyaada uchit hoga ki hamaare desh ke asli anndaata yahi chote kisaan hai
 These farmers have been destroyed by the weather
 aaj sarkaar hisaab laga rahi he ki kisaanon ko kya muaavja diya jaae
 The Central Government is putting the responsibility of the plight of the farmers at the Center and the State Governments at the states
 sansad main rahul gandhi, pradhanmantri narendra modi ko kisaanon ke bich jane kii salaah de rahe hai
 This pain of the political parties is increasing in the social media not only in the Parliament but for their own benefit
 modi ke videsh daure par sawaal uth rahe hai
 It means to say that the issue of ruined and dying farmers is becoming Rahul vs Modi
 jahaan tak kisaanon kii baat he to abhi tak unke nuksaan kaa survey tak nahin ho sakaa he
 By the time all this happens, the time to sow the next crop will come
 lekin ye fasal kaise boi jaaegi ye bada sawaal kisaanon ke saamne he
 Where will the devastated and ruined farmers raise money for the next crop seeds, manure, water and pesticides
 karj main dub chuke bhoomihin kisaanon ko agali kheti ke liye ab karj koun degaa? or pichhlaa karj wo kaise chukaayenge? kitni ladakiyon kii shaadiyaan tal jaaengi
 How many children will have to leave their studies
 kitne kisaan apana ghar-baar bechakar shaharon ke majdoor ban jaaenge
 The farmers are in so much pain that i and you will get tired of telling them, but their stories will not be reduced
 batiya or rehan par khet lekar guzar-basar karne vaale kisaanon kii sthiti to bhayaavah he
 Their deposits have gone
 karj bad chukaa he or khaane ke liye anaaj bhi nahin he
 And the cruel joke is that they will not even get compensation
 khet unke naam par nahin he or khet hi nahin hai to muaavja kaisaa? kitna vibhats he yah, iskaa andaja shaharon main rahane vaale log nahin laga sakate
 In such a situation, how will these farmers be provided relief? isi sawaal kaa jawaab jaanane ke liye ham pradhanmantri narendra modi ke sansadeey kshetra varanasi ke ek gaanv jagardevapur gaye
 But instead of getting answers there, many new questions were found
 hira laal is gaanv kii harijan basti se rahete hai
 He is landless and planted three bighas on potted area
 barish ne kuch nahin choda
 Hiralal has become ill in this sorrow
 charpai par lete rahete hai, lekin jab enditivi kii team inkaa haal jaanane pahunchi to yah kisi madad kii aas main uth khadey hue
 In summer, even after wearing a shawl, he walked towards the field apni barbaad fasal dikhaakar unhone apana gam bayaan kiya
 "the situation was one damme down ba, three bigha liye kulhi were destroyed
 ab hamen kaa mili kaa na mili wo t bataai dihe
 " gaanv ke malik yadav kaa bhi yahi haal he
 They had rented two bigha fields and are now trying to extract some workable material from the wasted grains
 unhone hamen bataaya ki kaise pani kii vajah se anaaj sad gaya he
 The same situation is with Salik Ram
 vahiin hamen barbaad fasal ko niharti piyaari bhi mili
 Piari has a wedding and the crop is ruined
 vah samaj nahin paa rahi he ki kya kare? saare raste band ho gaye hai
 "three big houses, we have taken the field, our house is quick, and our house is married
 ab i batai ham kekare boote biyah kari
 Everyone is crying at home
 he bhagwaan i kauna musiibat main daal dehala
 " rehan par kheti karne vaale kisaan chhunna laal hamen dekhakar is aas main daudte chale aae ki sahab aae hai
 Inspecting the wasted crop
 aate hi foran apane barbaad khet kii taraf chalane kii zid karne lage par jab hamane unase rehan khet lene waalon ke bare main poocha to foran fat pade, kaha sahab se mulaakaat ham khud rehan par khet liye hai
 The name of the farm
 adhiya vaale kheti kiye he jutai kiye he, benga daale he surra khaad daale he apana kharchaa laga diye hai unako kya milegaa
 The tenant will get it, what will we get? ham to mar jaaenge
 "comments jagardevapur samet banaras ke mahadaa, chakkaa, tilampur, namapur, wardih, khonchvaa, akhri chhitauni jaise saikadon gaanv main batiya or rehan par kheti karne vaale kisaan badahavaas hai
 Their biggest pain is that by raising money, somehow they did farming by borrowing and now when the crop is destroyed, they will not get compensation
 yahi nahin jisaki jameen he use rehan kii rakam to deni hi hogi
 Now they are on their mercy
 ye ek dardanaak sach he kyonki rehan or batiya par kheti karne vaale bhoomihin kisaanon kii zindagi jameen ke bina vaise bhi aadhi he or is baar kii barish ne unki sari mehnat dho di he
 Hence, his life has become completely lifeless
 bada sawaal ye he ki muaavjon kii list main kya aise kisaanon ko jagah milegi? ye kisaan sarkaar ke agenda main hai bhi yaa nahin? agar nahin to aap khud soch sakate hai ki ye kaise jinda rahenge or kisi tarah jinda bhi rahe to kis haal main jienge?
